Sanitize output: strip conversational preamble before gate validation\\n    _sanitize_output(step.output_file)\\n\\n    # Process completed successfully; gate check happens in execute_pipeline\\n    return StepResult(\\n        step=step,\\n        status=StepStatus.PASS,\\n        attempt=1,\\n        started_at=started_at,\\n        finished_at=finished_at,\\n    )\"}]"}}}

Uses atomic write (write to ``.tmp`` then ``os.replace()``) to prevent\n    partial file states.\n\n    Returns the byte count of the stripped preamble (0 when file already starts\n    with ``---`` or )\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n        extra_args = [\n            arg\n            for input_path in step.inputs\n            for arg in (\"--file\", str(input_path))\n        ]\n
